---
about_this_resource_text: <h2 class="subhead">Description</h2><p>In this lecture,
  Prof. Gruber takes what the class has already learned and applies it to more realistic
  situations, specifically monopoly profit maximization and welfare effects. See <a
  href="./resolveuid/e4635a413517f55c518f491dae1f8f0a">Handout 11</a> for relevant
  graphs for this lecture.&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Prof. Jonathan
  Gruber</p><p>&nbsp;</p>

  <span m="1603550">they</span> <span m="1603640">make</span> <span m="1603790">no</span>
  <span m="1603910">money.</span></p><p><span m="1605890">Monopolists</span> <span

  <span m="1611400">profit</span> <span m="1611760">maximization.</span> <span m="1613110">We</span>
  <span m="1613260">said</span> <span m="1613530">that</span> <span m="1613650">marginal</span>
  <span m="1614070">revenue</span> <span m="1614970">can</span> <span m="1615180">be</span>
  <span m="1615400">rewritten</span> <span m="1616530">as</span> <span m="1617220">price</span>

  <span m="1629490">we</span> <span m="1629610">can</span> <span m="1629790">rewrite</span>

  <span m="1631980">cost</span> <span m="1632370">over</span> <span m="1632580">price</span>
  <span m="1634330">equals</span> <span m="1635170">1</span> <span m="1635590">plus</span>
  <span m="1635980">1</span> <span m="1636310">over</span> <span m="1636520">the</span>
  <span m="1636640">elasticity</span> <span m="1637180">of</span> <span m="1637270">demand.</span>
  <span m="1640110">And</span> <span m="1640230">this</span> <span m="1640410">is</span>
  <span m="1640530">the</span> <span m="1640590">monopolist's</span> <span m="1641130">market</span>
  <span m="1641460">power</span> <span m="1641760">condition.</span> <span m="1643680">So</span>
  <span m="1643860">if</span> <span m="1643950">we</span> <span m="1644070">define</span>
  <span m="1644520">the</span> <span m="1644610">market--</span> <span m="1645400">so</span>

  <span m="1646110">something</span> <span m="1646890">we</span> <span m="1647040">call</span>

  <span m="1663200">the</span> <span m="1663290">price</span> <span m="1663770">is</span>

  <span m="2121250">exciting</span> <span m="2121610">moment</span> <span m="2122270">of</span>
